            <script>
window.gtmdataLayer = window.gtmdataLayer || [];
window.dlpush = gtmdataLayer.push;
gtmdataLayer.push = function(data) {
	if(data.event=='ADD_TO_BASKET' && data.products && data.products[0] && data.products[0].dimension21) {
		let score = data.products[0].dimension21.toUpperCase().charCodeAt(0) - 64;
		window._stsp=window._stsp||[];
		window._stsp.push({
			'event': 'nutriscore',
			'nutriscore':score
		});
    }
    return window.dlpush.apply(this, arguments);
};

</script>
<script>
window.ahDataLayer = window.ahDataLayer || null;

function detectUserType(item) {
    if(item.event!='cidDataLayerInitialized') return;
    if(!ahDataLayer) return;
    if(!ahDataLayer.data) return;
    if(!ahDataLayer.data.user) return;

    var sitespectEvent = {
        'event':'user-profile-event'
    };
    for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(ahDataLayer.data.user)) {
        if(!key.includes('gtm.') && !['digimon','idga','idmon'].includes(key))
        sitespectEvent[key] = value;
    }
    window._stsp=window._stsp||[];
    window._stsp.push(sitespectEvent);
}



window.gtmdataLayer = window.gtmdataLayer || [];
window.gtmdataLayer.forEach(detectUserType);
gtmdataLayer.detectUserTypePush = gtmdataLayer.push;
gtmdataLayer.push = function(item) {
    detectUserType(item);
    return gtmdataLayer.detectUserTypePush.apply(this, arguments);
};
</script><noscript><img src="https://www.ah.nl/akam/13/pixel_72bb4dfe?a=dD0zOGNhZTFmNDAxN2I1ZGE3NGI1MzA1ZDVkZDI1NTA2YjliOGYyNWI3JmpzPW9mZg==" style="visibility: hidden; position: absolute; left: -999px; top: -999px;" /></noscript><script type="text/javascript" nonce="e9dae644fb726ce57cacc48ab7d0f3f3" src="/9pV-K/D/JB/ewYH/-Zn0cjVy/NcO5JVhuuu1t/ZgZPJ2E8Bg/F3/NbPStvN18B?v=14be8ee6-ccb7-d1a0-d3c1-0385a5da5f65" defer></script></body>
